  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h1>Release Notes</h1>
<h2>Highlights</h2>
<ul>
<li>Multicopter hover thrust estimator (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="551948728" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13981" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981">#13981</a>)</li>
<li>Backup yaw estimator for emergency recovery (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="575101665" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/ecl/issues/766" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/ecl/pull/766/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/ecl/pull/766">PX4/ecl#766</a>)</li>
<li>new Invensense and Bosch IMU drivers enabled everywhere
<ul>
<li>completely rewritten drivers and framework optimized for flight performance (high rate raw data up to 8 kHz and low end-to-end latency)</li>
<li>configurable low latency sensor pipeline with new notch filter</li>
<li>Multicopter rate controller runs synchronized with primary gyro (up to 4 kHz configured via IMU_GYRO_RATEMAX)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Major sensor calibration improvements (<a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13632" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13632/hovercard">Gyro</a>, <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13623" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13623/hovercard">Mag</a>, <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13666" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13666/hovercard">Level</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Migration Guide</h3>
<ul>
<li>VTOL support is no longer included in flash limited px4_fmu-v2 hardware (original 3DR Pixhawk with silicon bug)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Hardware Support</h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="http://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_controller/durandal.html" rel="nofollow">Holybro Durandal</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="https://nxp.gitbook.io/ucans32k146/" rel="nofollow">NXP IMX-RT, S32K</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_controller/holybro_pix32_v5.html" rel="nofollow">Holybro PIX32V5</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_controller/cubepilot_cube_yellow.html" rel="nofollow">CubePilot Cube Yellow</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_controller/cubepilot_cube_orange.html" rel="nofollow">CubePilot Cube Orange</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://doc.cuav.net/flight-controller/x7/en/" rel="nofollow">CUAV X7</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://doc.cuav.net/flight-controller/x7/en/x7-pro.html" rel="nofollow">CUAV X7 Pro</a>, (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
<li><a href="http://doc.cuav.net/flight-controller/x7/en/nora.html" rel="nofollow">CUAV Nora</a>, (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="677803023" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/15536" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/15536/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/15536">#15536</a>) (Manufacturer Supported)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Drivers</h3>
<ul>
<li>SPI DMA adds centralized DMA map (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569287363" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14207" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14207/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14207">#14207</a>)</li>
<li>Move primary IMU to new InvenSense driver (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="578963028" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14356" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14356/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14356">#14356</a>)</li>
<li>New drivers interface and consolidation (PR  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="580479716" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14386" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14386/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14386">#14386</a> )</li>
</ul>
<h3>System Architecture</h3>
<ul>
<li>Board config simplifications for SPI &amp; I2C (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569963544" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14221" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14221/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14221">#14221</a>) and PWM timers (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="545863072" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13871" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13871/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13871">#13871</a>)</li>
<li>Adds UAVCAN node <code>cannode</code> (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="564445962" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14148" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14148/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14148">#14148</a>)</li>
<li>Adds CAN interface runtime (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="579422962" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14367" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14367/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14367">#14367</a>)</li>
<li>Support for multiple UAVCAN v0.1 Smart Batteries (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="568779441" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14198" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14198/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14198">#14198</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Multicopter</h3>
<ul>
<li>New hover thrust estimator (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="551948728" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13981" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981">#13981</a>)</li>
<li>XYZ-synchronized motion in auto modes (diagonal climb) (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="528655275" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13596" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13596/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13596">#13596</a>)</li>
<li>New Notch filter (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="526495644" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13549" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13549/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13549">#13549</a>)</li>
<li>Acceleration feedforward (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569373004" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14212" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14212/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14212">#14212</a>)</li>
<li>Mag power compensation (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="586099460" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14457" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14457/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14457">#14457</a>, <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/advanced_config/compass_power_compensation.html" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>

<h3>OS/NuttX</h3>
<p>The release includes a change from <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/101f3bddecb70cfb8dc78c5b4fad98f3480ae399/ReleaseNotes#lines-21789" rel="nofollow">NuttX-7.29 </a> to <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/efff9b9438e69ea6c70e879b7ee4d49bff1b0988/ReleaseNotes#lines-25651" rel="nofollow">NuttX-8.2</a><br>
See <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/efff9b9438e69ea6c70e879b7ee4d49bff1b0988/ReleaseNotes#lines-25651" rel="nofollow">NuttX release notes</a> for the details of changes in NuttX-8.2 details.</p>
<p>Included as backports are:</p>
<ul>
<li>STM32[F4 F7 H7]
<ul>
<li>spi_exchange (no DMA) with for STM32xx_SPI_DMATHRESHOLD</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>STM32[F7 H7]
<ul>
<li>SDMMC internal pull up usage fixed</li>
<li>Add check_format tooling</li>
<li>nxstyle - output compiler like error format</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>STM32H7
<ul>
<li>fix stm32h7x3xx_dmamux.h: add missing underscore to defines</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>STM32F7
<ul>
<li>stm32f7:Add Serial Tx DMA</li>
<li>stm32f7:ethernet: Add some delays so that ifup() does not</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>NXP IMX-RT, S32K
<ul>
<li>S32K add support for Nxp drone boards</li>
<li>imxrt: Adds the ability to run from OCRAM</li>
<li>imxrt: Add USB Device support for i.MX RT</li>
<li>imxrt: added missing i2c prescale mask</li>
<li>imxrt: interrupt serial storm, add DTCM and set up I and</li>
<li>imxrt: Allow clock setting for SPI and I2C from board.h.</li>
<li>imxrt:lpi2c Fix interrupt storm on failed write.</li>
<li>imxrt:lpi2c ensure that on an error status reflects it.</li>
<li>imxrt:lpi2c imxrt_lpi2c_reset uses GPIO with SION</li>
<li>imxrt:gpio Support readback on OUT GPIO</li>
<li>imxrt1020-evk: Enable the GPIO based CD.</li>
<li>imxrt:lpspi: Fixed race on register setting.</li>
<li>imxrt:lpspi: Remove hack setting LPSPI1 daisy irrespective</li>
<li>imxrt:lpi2c.c:Added configurations to fine tune LPI2C Time</li>
<li>IMXRT106x USDHC: Support regular GPIO for CD and inversion.</li>
<li>IMXRT106x:pinout add ALT 8 GPIO_GPT2_COMPARE3 &amp; fix GPIO_G</li>
<li>IMXRT106x:pinout add ALT 8 GPIO_GPT1_CAPTURE[1|2]</li>
<li>Kinetis renamed TJA1100 to TJA110X registers</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h1>v1.11 Release Notes</h1>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>New significantly improved Invensense IMU drivers that provide all raw data up to 8 kHz using SPI DMA.
<ul>
<li>rate controller can run up to 2 kHz (&gt;= 4 kHz coming soon) by setting<code>IMU_GYRO_RATEMAX</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>New multicopter hover thrust estimator (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="551948728" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13981" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981">#13981</a>)</li>
<li>Emergency Yaw recovery using EKF-GSF estimator (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="575101665" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/ecl/issues/766" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/ecl/pull/766/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/ecl/pull/766">PX4/ecl#766</a>)</li>
<li>Major sensor calibration improvements (<a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13632" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13632/hovercard">Gyro</a>, <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13623" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13623/hovercard">Mag</a>, <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13666" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13666/hovercard">Level</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Main Features and Improvements</h3>
<h3>Migration Guide</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>DEPRECATED:</strong> VTOL is no longer supported in FMUv2 hardware</li>
</ul>
<h3>PX4/Drivers</h3>
<ul>
<li>Enable SPI DMA adds centralized DMA map (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569287363" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14207" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14207/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14207">#14207</a>)</li>
<li>Move primary IMU to new InvenSense driver (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="578963028" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14356" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14356/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14356">#14356</a>)
<ul>
<li>FMUv5, FMUv5x</li>
<li>ModalAI_fv-v1</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Drivers CLI interface consolidation (PR  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="580479716" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14386" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14386/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14386">#14386</a> )</li>
</ul>
<h3>System Architecture</h3>
<ul>
<li>Board config simplifications for SPI &amp; I2C (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569963544" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14221" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14221/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14221">#14221</a>) and PWM timers (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="545863072" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13871" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13871/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13871">#13871</a>)</li>
<li>Adds UAVCAN node <code>cannode</code> (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="564445962" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14148" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14148/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14148">#14148</a>)</li>
<li>Adds CAN interface runtime (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="579422962" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14367" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14367/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14367">#14367</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>Multicopter</h3>
<ul>
<li>New hover thrust estimator (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="551948728" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13981" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13981">#13981</a>)</li>
<li>XYZ-synchronized motion in auto modes (diagonal climb)</li>
<li>New Notch filter (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="526495644" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13549" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13549/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13549">#13549</a>)</li>
<li>Acceleration feedforward (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569373004" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14212" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14212/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14212">#14212</a>)</li>
<li>Mag power compensation (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="586099460" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14457" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14457/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14457">#14457</a>, <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/advanced_config/compass_power_compensation.html" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>Takeoff failure detection (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="584411490" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/14428" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/14428/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/14428">#14428</a>, <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/config/safety.html#failure_detector" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>Horizontal velocity limit close to ground (PR <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="527102989" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/issues/13561" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13561/hovercard" href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13561">#13561</a>, <a href="https://dev.px4.io/master/en/advanced/parameter_reference.html#MPC_LAND_VEL_XY" rel="nofollow">Parameter</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3>VTOL</h3>
<ul>

    <relative-time datetime="2020-01-21T20:40:18Z" class="no-wrap">Jan 21, 2020</relative-time>
    &middot;

    3055 commits</a>
    to master
    since this release
</p>
    </div>

    

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <p>This point release reduces the CPU load on FMUv2/v3 targets by setting the default rate control loop executing speed to 400 Hz. The v1.10 release increases the default rate control speed from 250 Hz (v1.9 and before) to 1000 Hz (v1.10), which not all boards can sustain in terms of CPU speed.</p>
  </div>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>Release Notes</h2>
<h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li>Multicopter 1 kHz rate loop (param IMU_GYRO_RATEMAX)</li>
<li>DShot ESC Support with Telemetry (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12854" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12854/hovercard">#12854</a>, <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/peripherals/dshot.html" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>Cone-based RTL (<a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_modes/return.html#return_altitude" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>Significantly improved real time system performance
<ul>
<li>new work queue scheduling framework with a thread per physical bus</li>
<li>new C++ uORB API (faster, safer, and more memory efficient)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>new RTF airframes
<ul>
<li>Holybro Kopis 2 (and KakuteF7 board)</li>
<li>Holybro S500</li>
<li>UVify Draco</li>
<li>UVify Draco-R</li>
<li>UVify IFO</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>NuttX RTOS upgrade with a number of important bug fixes and performance improvements</li>
</ul>
<h3>Additional Features and Improvements</h3>
<h4>Migration Guide</h4>
<ul>
<li>DEPRECATED: Throttle PID Attenuation (TPA) (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13208" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13208/hovercard">#13208</a>)
<ul>
<li>Deprecated in favor of <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/config_mc/pid_tuning_guide_multicopter.html#thrust_curve" rel="nofollow">Thrust Curve</a> compensation.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4>Multicopter</h4>
<ul>
<li>the rate controller now runs synchronized with the primary gyro</li>
<li>Rate integrator improvements (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12296" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12296/hovercard">#12296</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>VTOL</h4>
<ul>
<li>VTOL front transition heading handling improvements (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12630" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12630/hovercard">#12630</a>)</li>
<li>RTL: By default enable return via landing pattern for deterministic back-transition (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12746" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12746/hovercard">#12746</a>)</li>
<li>VTOL GPS fix bank loiter (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12778" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12778/hovercard">#12778</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>Fixed Wing</h4>
<ul>
<li>initial support for new airspeed selector module capable of detecting airspeed sensor faults</li>
</ul>
<h4>Rover</h4>
<ul>
<li>Enable Offboard support for Rover position control</li>
</ul>
<h4>PX4/ECL - Estimators improvement</h4>
<ul>
<li>many bug fixes and robustness improvements</li>
<li>Mag inconsistency check (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12334" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12334/hovercard">#12334</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>PX4/Drivers</h4>
<ul>
<li>UAVCAN sensor drivers for battery and optical flow</li>
</ul>
<h4>Computer Vision &amp; Autonomy</h4>
<h5>PX4/Avoidance</h5>
<ul>
<li>Safe Landing Planner support</li>
<li>Collision Prevention Improvements</li>
</ul>
<h4>Simulation</h4>
<ul>
<li>Simulation-In-Hardware (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/11835" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/11835/hovercard">#11835</a>, <a href="https://dev.px4.io/master/en/simulation/simulation-in-hardware.html" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>jMAVSim headless/no-GUI option (jMAVSim <a href="https://github.com/PX4/jMAVSim/pull/105" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/jMAVSim/pull/105/hovercard">PR #105</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>Logging improvements</h4>
<ul>
<li>AUX1-RC-channel-based logging via SDLOG_MODE (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12100" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12100/hovercard">#12100</a>)</li>
<li>Logging of system bootup messages, and dmesg tool (on boards with enough RAM) (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/11792" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/11792/hovercard">#11792</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>Onboard computer / middleware improvements</h4>
<h4>Failsafe / commander improvements</h4>
<ul>
<li>Bugfixes for failsafe corner cases (PRs <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13143" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13143/hovercard">#13143</a>, <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/13294" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/13294/hovercard">#13294</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h4>OS/NuttX</h4>
<p>The release includes a change from <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/48d1d9d84f18461aba2eeaf39cae3aafce2fce4d/ReleaseNotes#lines-20687" rel="nofollow">NuttX-7.28 </a> to <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/101f3bddecb70cfb8dc78c5b4fad98f3480ae399/ReleaseNotes#lines-21789" rel="nofollow">NuttX-7.29</a><br>
See <a href="https://bitbucket.org/nuttx/nuttx/src/101f3bddecb70cfb8dc78c5b4fad98f3480ae399/ReleaseNotes#lines-21789" rel="nofollow">NuttX release notes</a> for the details of changes in NuttX-7.29 details.</p>
<p>Included as backports are:</p>
<ul>
<li>STM32F7 I2C state and interrupt storm fixes.</li>
<li>Serial Single wire mode has moved to NuttX</li>
<li>Fix for "z" in printf</li>
<li>kinetis:i2c transfer ensure correct result returned.</li>
<li>kinetis_i2c_transfer released the mutex then fetched the state, this resulted in returning the correct results.</li>
<li>STM32F4 and STM32F7 SD card hang on card eject fixed</li>
<li>STM32F7 ethernet add timeout on MAC reset</li>
</ul>
<h4>Updated Supported Hardware</h4>
<ul>
<li>Holybro Kakute F7 board support (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12440" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12440/hovercard">#12440</a>, <a href="https://docs.px4.io/master/en/flight_controller/kakutef7.html" rel="nofollow">Docs</a>)</li>
<li>Kopis 2 Airframe configuration (PR <a href="https://github.com/PX4/Firmware/pull/12549" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/PX4/Firmware/pull/12549/hovercard">#12549</a>)</li>
</ul>
